????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????????   12. logoutAction [logout] 
    	"ChemoJunSystem logoutAction."

	ObjectMemory globalGarbageCollect.
	^self
  13. makeRuntimeImage1 [runtime] 
    	"ChemoJunSystem makeRuntimeImage1."

	| aStream imageMakerClass |
	(ObjectMemory versionId at: 5) >= 72 ifTrue: [^nil].
	aStream := WriteStream on: (String new: 16).
	aStream 
		nextPutAll: (#jun_Did_you_save_your_image_file_ 
				>> 'Did you save your image file?') asString.
	aStream cr.
	aStream 
		nextPutAll: (#jun__Smalltalk_quits_after____ime_image_are_created__ 
				>> '(Smalltalk quits after the run time image are created).') asString.
	(JunDialog confirm: aStream contents initialAnswer: false) 
		ifFalse: [^self].
	(PCFilename fileSystems includesKey: 'FAT32') 
		ifFalse: [PCFilename fileSystems at: 'FAT32' put: FATFilename].
	(PCFilename fileSystems includesKey: 'UDFFS') 
		ifFalse: [PCFilename fileSystems at: 'UDFFS' put: FATFilename].
	ScheduledWindow promptForOpen: false.
	JunTranscriptFile uninstall.
	JunImageDispenser default flushCachedImages.
	ScheduledControllers scheduledControllers do: 
			[:controller | 
			((controller model isKindOf: JunLauncher) 
				or: [controller model isKindOf: ChemoJunLauncher]) 
					ifTrue: [controller closeAndUnschedule]].
	JunApplicationModel displayPendingInvalidation.
	Cursor wait showWhile: 
			[ExternalDictionary 
				allInstancesDo: [:each | each fillDefineCachesWithValues]].
	JunLauncher disableOnRunTime.
	ChemoJunLauncher enableOnRunTime.
	(ObjectMemory versionId at: 5) >= 70 
		ifTrue: [Parcel ensureLoadedParcel: 'ImageMaker' withVersion: '7']
		ifFalse: [Parcel ensureLoadedParcel: 'ImageMaker' withVersion: '5i'].
	imageMakerClass := nil.
	SystemUtils allBehaviorsDo: 
			[:aClass | 
			aClass name = #ImageMaker ifTrue: [imageMakerClass := aClass]].
	imageMakerClass isNil ifFalse: [imageMakerClass open]
  14. makeRuntimeImage2 [runtime] 
    	"ChemoJunSystem makeRuntimeImage2."

	| runtimeBuilderClass aStream runtimeBuilder options keptItems settingBlock |
	(ObjectMemory versionId at: 5) < 72 ifTrue: [^nil].
	Parcel ensureLoadedParcel: 'RuntimePackager' withVersion: '7.4'.
	runtimeBuilderClass := nil.
	SystemUtils allBehaviorsDo: 
			[:aClass | 
			aClass name = #RuntimeBuilderUI ifTrue: [runtimeBuilderClass := aClass]].
	runtimeBuilderClass isNil ifTrue: [^nil].
	aStream := WriteStream on: (String new: 16).
	aStream 
		nextPutAll: (#jun_Did_you_save_your_image_file_ 
				>> 'Did you save your image file?') asString.
	aStream cr.
	aStream 
		nextPutAll: (#jun__Smalltalk_quits_after____ime_image_are_created__ 
				>> '(Smalltalk quits after the run time image are created).') asString.
	(JunDialog confirm: aStream contents initialAnswer: false) ifFalse: [^nil].
	"----- Make Runtime Image -----"
	(PCFilename fileSystems includesKey: 'FAT32') 
		ifFalse: [PCFilename fileSystems at: 'FAT32' put: FATFilename].
	(PCFilename fileSystems includesKey: 'UDFFS') 
		ifFalse: [PCFilename fileSystems at: 'UDFFS' put: FATFilename].
	ScheduledWindow promptForOpen: false.
	JunTranscriptFile uninstall.
	JunImageDispenser default flushCachedImages.
	ScheduledControllers scheduledControllers do: 
			[:controller | 
			((controller model isKindOf: JunLauncher) 
				or: [controller model isKindOf: ChemoJunLauncher]) 
					ifTrue: [controller closeAndUnschedule]].
	JunApplicationModel displayPendingInvalidation.
	Cursor wait showWhile: 
			[ExternalDictionary 
				allInstancesDo: [:each | each fillDefineCachesWithValues]].
	JunLauncher disableOnRunTime.
	ChemoJunLauncher enableOnRunTime.
	"----- Setting Runtime Builder -----"
	runtimeBuilder := runtimeBuilderClass new.
	options := runtimeBuilder 
				instVarAt: (runtimeBuilder class allInstVarNames indexOf: 'options').
	options startupClass: ChemoJun.ChemoJunLauncher.
	options startupMethod: #install.
	options imagePath: ChemoJunSystem system , ChemoJunSystem version , 'RT'.
	keptItems := runtimeBuilder 
				instVarAt: (runtimeBuilder class allInstVarNames indexOf: 'keptItems').
	settingBlock := 
			[:nameSpace :classCollection | 
			keptItems keptClasses addAll: classCollection.
			classCollection 
				do: [:each | keptItems deletedClasses remove: each ifAbsent: [nil]].
			keptItems keptGlobals addAll: (nameSpace dataBindings 
						collect: [:each | BindingReference pathString: nameSpace fullName , '.' , each key]).
			keptItems keptMethods 
				addAll: 
					[| aCollection |
					aCollection := List new: classCollection size * 2.
					classCollection do: 
							[:each | 
							aCollection add: each -> each selectors.
							aCollection add: each class -> each class selectors].
					aCollection yourself] 
							value].
	"----- Setting OS -----"
	settingBlock value: OS value: OS classes.
	"----- Setting Jun -----"
	settingBlock value: Jun value: JunSystem classes.
	"----- Setting HaptiChem -----"
	settingBlock value: ChemoJun value: ChemoJunSystem classes.
	"----- Runtime Packager Open -----"
	runtimeBuilder open.
	^runtimeBuilder
  15. postLoadParcel: aParcel [parcel] 
     
	"This method will be hooked after ChemoJun parcel loading."

	self releaseVersionOfSmalltalk >= 74 
		ifTrue: 
			[| definedClasses |
			definedClasses := aParcel definedClasses.
			(definedClasses select: [:aClass | definedClasses includes: aClass]) do: 
					[:aClass | 
					(aClass superclass subclasses includes: aClass) 
						ifFalse: [aClass superclass addSubclass: aClass]]].
	self releaseVersionOfSmalltalk >= 50 
		ifTrue: 
			[Compiler 
				evaluate: 'Smalltalk addImport: (GeneralNameSpaceImport path: #(''ChemoJun'' ''*''))'].
	self install
  16. preUnloadParcel: aParcel [parcel] 
     
	| classes |
	(ObjectMemory dependents includes: self soleSystem) 
		ifTrue: [ObjectMemory removeDependent: self soleSystem].
	"self uninstallFont."
	self classes do: 
			[:each | 
			((each = self) not and: [each class includesSelector: #uninstall]) 
				ifTrue: 
					[Transcript
						cr;
						show: each name asString , ' uninstall ... '.
					each uninstall.
					Transcript
						show: 'done.';
						flush]].
	classes := self classes reverse.
	ScheduledControllers scheduledControllers do: 
			[:controller | 
			classes do: 
					[:each | 
					(controller view model isKindOf: each) 
						ifTrue: [controller closeAndUnschedule]]].
	ObjectMemory globalGarbageCollect.
	self releaseVersionOfSmalltalk >= 50 
		ifTrue: 
			[Compiler 
				evaluate: 'Smalltalk removeImport: (GeneralNameSpaceImport path: #(''ChemoJun'' ''*''))']
  17. projectNameString [logo] 
    	^(#chemoJun_ChemoJun_Project >> 'ChemoJun Project') asString
  18. prologueAction [login] 
    	"ChemoJunSystem prologueAction."

	self aboutForSeconds: 3.
	^self
  19. propagateCopyright [copyright] 
    	"ChemoJunSystem propagateCopyright."

	| copyright comment category stream |
	copyright := self copyright.
	comment := self copyrightString.
	category := #copyright.
	(self classes asSortedCollection: [:a :b | a name < b name]) do: 
			[:each | 
			each comment: comment.
			each = self 
				ifFalse: 
					[stream := WriteStream on: String new.
					stream nextPutAll: 'copyright'.
					stream cr.
					stream tab.
					stream nextPutAll: '^'.
					stream nextPutAll: copyright printString.
					each class compile: stream contents classified: category.
					stream := WriteStream on: String new.
					stream nextPutAll: 'system'.
					stream cr.
					stream tab.
					stream nextPutAll: '^'.
					stream nextPutAll: self system printString.
					each class compile: stream contents classified: category.
					stream := WriteStream on: String new.
					stream nextPutAll: 'version'.
					stream cr.
					stream tab.
					stream nextPutAll: '^'.
					stream nextPutAll: self version printString.
					stream cr.
					each class compile: stream contents classified: category.
					Transcript
						cr;
						show: each class printString , ' < copyright'].
			self sortProtocols: each.
			self sortProtocols: each class].
	((Smalltalk includesKey: #ChemoJun) 
		and: [(Smalltalk at: #ChemoJun) respondsTo: #comment:]) 
			ifTrue: [(Smalltalk at: #ChemoJun) comment: self copyrightString]
  20. readChemoJunEnvironment [private] 
    	"ChemoJunSystem readChemoJunEnvironment."

	| aDictionary aFilename aStream aString aCollection aKey aValue anIndex |
	aDictionary := Dictionary new.
	aFilename := 'ChemoJunSetEnv.txt' asFilename.
	aFilename exists ifFalse: [^aDictionary].
	aFilename isReadable ifFalse: [^aDictionary].
	aStream := aFilename readStream.
	
	[[aStream atEnd] whileFalse: 
			[aString := JunStringUtility getLine: aStream.
			aCollection := JunStringUtility separate: aString
						dividers: JunStringUtility separators.
			(aCollection size >= 3 and: [aCollection first asLowercase = 'setenv']) 
				ifTrue: 
					[aKey := aCollection at: 2.
					aValue := aString 
								copyFrom: (aString findString: (aCollection at: 3) startingAt: 1)
								to: aString size.
					anIndex := aValue reverse 
								findFirst: [:aCharacter | aCharacter isSeparator not].
					anIndex > 0 
						ifTrue: [aValue := aValue copyFrom: 1 to: aValue size - (anIndex - 1)].
					aValue size >= 2 
						ifTrue: 
							[((aValue first = $' and: [aValue last = $']) 
								or: [aValue first = $" and: [aValue last = $"]]) 
									ifTrue: [aValue := aValue copyFrom: 2 to: aValue size - 1]].
					aDictionary at: aKey put: aValue]]] 
			ensure: [aStream close].
	^aDictionary
  21. reportWriter [reporting] 
    	| htmlReportWriter |
	htmlReportWriter := JunHtmlReportWriter 
				name: self system , self version , '-Report'
				categories: #('ChemoJun-*')
				filter: 
					[:aClass | 
					| string |
					string := aClass name asString.
					string := string copyFrom: 1
								to: (self system asString size min: string size).
					string = self system asString].
	^htmlReportWriter
  22. saveAsParcel [parcel] 
    	"ChemoJunSystem saveAsParcel."

	| aParcel |
	aParcel := Parcel parcelNamed: self system.
	aParcel isNil ifTrue: [aParcel := Parcel createParcelNamed: self system].
	aParcel isEmpty ifTrue: [^nil].
	aParcel comment: self system , self version , ' (' , self date , ') '.
	aParcel version: self version.
	aParcel prerequisiteParcels: (Array 
				with: (Array with: JunSystem system with: JunSystem version)).
	aParcel 
		postLoadBlock: '[:aParcel | (aParcel definedClasses detect: [:c | c name = ' 
				, self name asSymbol printString , ']) postLoadParcel: aParcel]'.
	aParcel 
		preUnloadBlock: '[:aParcel | (aParcel definedClasses detect: [:c | c name = ' 
				, self name asSymbol printString , ']) preUnloadParcel: aParcel]'.
	aParcel 
		parcelOutOn: self system , self version , '.pcl'
		withSource: self system , self version , '.pst'
		hideOnLoad: false
		republish: false
		backup: false
  23. sourceCodeSaver [saving] 
    	"ChemoJunSystem sourceCodeSaver."

	| sourceCodeSaver |
	sourceCodeSaver := JunSourceCodeSaver 
				name: self system , self version
				categories: #('ChemoJun-*')
				filter: 
					[:aClass | 
					| string |
					string := aClass name asString.
					string := string copyFrom: 1
								to: (self system asString size min: string size).
					string = self system asString].
	sourceCodeSaver header: '
Smalltalk addImport: (GeneralNameSpaceImport path: #(''ChemoJun'' ''*''))
'.
	sourceCodeSaver footer: 'ChemoJunSystem install.'.
	sourceCodeSaver parcel: 'ChemoJun'.
	sourceCodeSaver namespace: ChemoJun.
	sourceCodeSaver 
		prerequisite: 'Parcel ensureLoadedParcel: ''' , JunSystem system 
				, ''' withVersion: ''' , JunSystem version 
				, ''''.
	sourceCodeSaver environment: ChemoJun unambiguousName.
	^sourceCodeSaver
  24. system [copyright] 
    	^'ChemoJun' copy
  25. uninstall [class initialization] 
    	"ChemoJunSystem uninstall."

	| classes categories block |
	(Dialog confirm: 'Do you want to uninstall?' initialAnswer: false) 
		ifFalse: [^self].
	(ObjectMemory dependents includes: self soleSystem) 
		ifTrue: [ObjectMemory removeDependent: self soleSystem].
	self classes do: 
			[:each | 
			((each = self) not and: [each class includesSelector: #uninstall]) 
				ifTrue: 
					[Transcript
						cr;
						show: each name asString , ' uninstall ... '.
					each uninstall.
					Transcript
						show: 'done.';
						flush]].
	classes := self classes reverse.
	categories := Set new.
	classes do: [:each | categories add: each category].
	categories := categories asSortedCollection.
	ScheduledControllers scheduledControllers do: 
			[:controller | 
			classes do: 
					[:each | 
					(controller view model isKindOf: each) 
						ifTrue: [controller closeAndUnschedule]]].
	block := 
			[classes do: 
					[:each | 
					| string |
					string := each printString.
					each removeFromSystem.
					Transcript
						cr;
						show: 'removed ' , string].
			ObjectMemory globalGarbageCollect.
			categories do: 
					[:each | 
					| elements |
					elements := Smalltalk organization listAtCategoryNamed: each asSymbol.
					elements isEmpty 
						ifTrue: 
							[Smalltalk organization removeCategory: each asSymbol.
							Transcript
								cr;
								show: 'removed ' , each asString]].
			ObjectMemory globalGarbageCollect
			"Browser withAllSubclasses do: [:each | each allInstances do: [:it | it updateCategories]]"].
	[Cursor wait showWhile: [block value]] fork
  26. upgrade [saving] 
    	"ChemoJunSystem upgrade."

	self browseUnparceledMethodsOfDefinedClasses ifNotNil: [:browser | ^nil].
	self propagateCopyright.
	self errorSignal handle: [:exception | exception return]
		do: [self sortCatalogFileForJapanese].
	self save.
	self report.
	"self encyclopedia."
	self errorSignal handle: [:exception | ^JunVersionBrowser open]
		do: 
			[self 
				vdb: self system
				from: '021'
				to: self version].
	^self yourself
  27. version [copyright] 
    	^'050' copy
